Clean-room original question bank

SQE1 원문복제없는 문제집 v0.2

이 문제집은 공식 SQE/SRA 자료와 공개 법령·판례 출처를 기준으로 만든 original question bank입니다. 유료 교재, 유료 문제은행, 비공개 기출·복원문제를 복제하지 않았습니다.

공식 sample questions는 full mock이 아니라 유형·난이도·시간 압박을 확인하는 자료입니다. 이 문제집은 그 원칙을 반영해 stem, lead-in, five options 구조로 훈련하도록 만들었습니다.

생성일: 2026-07-03 | 목표: 2027년 1월 SQE1 대비용 original drill and mock workbook
SQE1 Workbook v0.2 | Cover
Assessment intelligence

공식 통계에서 가져온 훈련 원칙

공식 SQE sample question 안내와 SQE reports 목록은 문제풀이 훈련의 방향을 정하는 데 유용합니다. 숫자는 암기할 대상이 아니라, 훈련 강도를 조절하는 기준입니다.

  • 각 FLK는 180개의 single best answer MCQ로 구성됩니다.
  • 각 세션은 90문항, 2시간 33분 구조이므로 평균 약 1.7분에 한 문제를 처리해야 합니다.
  • 공식 sample questions는 전체 범위를 덮는 full mock이 아니므로, 별도 문제은행과 약점 반복이 필요합니다.
  • 문항과 선택지는 sitting마다 무작위화될 수 있으므로, 번호나 순서가 아니라 rule-trigger를 기준으로 푸는 습관이 필요합니다.
  • pass mark는 sitting별 난이도를 고려해 정해지므로, 고정 점수보다 상대적으로 안정적인 정답률을 목표로 해야 합니다.
훈련 기준: 처음에는 정답률 55%를 넘기는 것보다 오답 원인을 R/F/E/P/ETH로 분류하는 것이 중요합니다. 이후 65%, 72%, 80% 단계로 올립니다.
SQE1 Workbook v0.2 | Official data method
Error taxonomy

오답 기록 코드

코드의미처방
RRule gaprule sheet로 돌아가 요건을 한 문장으로 다시 쓴다.
FFact readingstem에서 당사자, 단계, 문서, 기한, 돈을 표시한다.
EEnglish/legal term영국법 용어를 한국어 감각으로 오역했는지 확인한다.
PProcedure지금 단계에서 가능한 조치인지 다시 본다.
ETHEthicsSRA Principles, Code, Accounts Rules overlay를 확인한다.
SQE1 Workbook v0.2 | Error taxonomy
FLK1

Workbook Chapter 1. Legal System of England and Wales

이 장은 Legal System of England and Wales 문제풀이 장입니다. 목표는 지식을 많이 읽는 것이 아니라, 제한시간 안에서 trigger를 보고 바로 rule을 꺼내는 것입니다.

오늘의 목표

  1. 핵심 쟁점 6개를 문제로 확인한다.
  2. 짧은 issue drill과 긴 fact-pattern drill을 모두 푼다.
  3. 오답을 R/F/E/P/ETH 코드로 분류한다.
문항은 모두 새로 만든 연습문제입니다. 공식 sample question이나 유료 문제은행의 문항·선택지·해설을 복제하지 않습니다.
SQE1 Workbook v0.2 | Legal System of England and Wales | intro
FLK1

Legal System of England and Wales Questions 1-3

Q1. Sources of law

A client scenario in Legal System of England and Wales contains the following clues: statute, regulation, guidance, case, tribunal. Which option is the best SQE1 method?

  1. Take the step the client prefers because client instructions decide the answer.
  2. Use the clues (statute, regulation, guidance, case, tribunal) to apply this rule: Primary legislation, delegated legislation and binding precedent do different jobs. First identify the source before applying it.
  3. Identify the precise rule, apply it to the stated facts, and check procedure and ethics before selecting the best answer.
  4. Use the Korean-law equivalent unless the question expressly warns that England and Wales differs.
  5. Delay the answer because SQE1 questions never require practical advice.
Q2. Sources of law

A client scenario in Legal System of England and Wales contains the following clues: statute, regulation, guidance, case, tribunal. Which option is the best SQE1 method?

  1. Take the step the client prefers because client instructions decide the answer.
  2. Choose the answer that states a broad legal principle without testing the facts.
  3. Use the clues (statute, regulation, guidance, case, tribunal) to apply this rule: Primary legislation, delegated legislation and binding precedent do different jobs. First identify the source before applying it.
  4. Use the Korean-law equivalent unless the question expressly warns that England and Wales differs.
  5. Delay the answer because SQE1 questions never require practical advice.
Q3. Sources of law

A solicitor is advising a client on a matter involving Legal System of England and Wales. The file contains a hurried email from the client, an incomplete chronology, and a document that may change the legal analysis. The strongest clues are: statute, regulation, guidance, case, tribunal. The supervising partner asks what should be done first, bearing in mind Human Rights Act 1998 and the need to avoid misleading the client or another party.

  1. Give the commercially attractive conclusion immediately, because speed is the main professional duty.
  2. Ignore the incomplete fact because all SQE1 questions are designed to test only black-letter recall.
  3. Identify the rule family, isolate the missing fact, then advise only on the legally available next step.
  4. Apply the rule on Sources of law: Primary legislation, delegated legislation and binding precedent do different jobs. First identify the source before applying it. Then test whether the missing fact or ethics point changes the next step.
  5. Choose the option that would be correct if the matter were governed by Korean law.

Legal System of England and Wales Questions 4-6

Q4. Precedent

A client scenario in Legal System of England and Wales contains the following clues: ratio, obiter, Court of Appeal, Supreme Court. Which option is the best SQE1 method?

  1. Take the step the client prefers because client instructions decide the answer.
  2. Choose the answer that states a broad legal principle without testing the facts.
  3. Use the clues (ratio, obiter, Court of Appeal, Supreme Court) to apply this rule: The ratio of a higher court binds lower courts; obiter and decisions from other hierarchies may persuade but do not bind in the same way.
  4. Use the Korean-law equivalent unless the question expressly warns that England and Wales differs.
  5. Delay the answer because SQE1 questions never require practical advice.

Legal System of England and Wales Answer Key

정답표입니다. 맞힌 문제도 해설을 읽고, 왜 다른 선택지가 best answer가 아닌지 한 문장으로 말합니다.

No.AnsIssueTeaching explanation
1 B Sources of law The trap is: Treating guidance or policy as if it were automatically binding law. The SQE1 answer must fit the facts, the procedural or transactional stage, and any professional conduct overlay.
2 C Sources of law The trap is: Treating guidance or policy as if it were automatically binding law. The SQE1 answer must fit the facts, the procedural or transactional stage, and any professional conduct overlay.
3 D Sources of law This is a longer fact-pattern drill. The correct method is to spot Sources of law, resist the trap (Treating guidance or policy as if it were automatically binding law.), and choose the best legally available step.
4 C Precedent The trap is: Selecting the answer with a famous case name without checking the court hierarchy. The SQE1 answer must fit the facts, the procedural or transactional stage, and any professional conduct overlay.
5 D Precedent The trap is: Selecting the answer with a famous case name without checking the court hierarchy. The SQE1 answer must fit the facts, the procedural or transactional stage, and any professional conduct overlay.
6 E Precedent This is a longer fact-pattern drill. The correct method is to spot Precedent, resist the trap (Selecting the answer with a famous case name without checking the court hierarchy.), and choose the best legally available step.
7 D Statutory interpretation The trap is: Ignoring the definition section or reading a lay meaning into a legal term. The SQE1 answer must fit the facts, the procedural or transactional stage, and any professional conduct overlay.
8 E Statutory interpretation The trap is: Ignoring the definition section or reading a lay meaning into a legal term. The SQE1 answer must fit the facts, the procedural or transactional stage, and any professional conduct overlay.
9 A Statutory interpretation This is a longer fact-pattern drill. The correct method is to spot Statutory interpretation, resist the trap (Ignoring the definition section or reading a lay meaning into a legal term.), and choose the best legally available step.
10 E Court structure The trap is: Assuming every important case starts in the High Court. The SQE1 answer must fit the facts, the procedural or transactional stage, and any professional conduct overlay.
11 A Court structure The trap is: Assuming every important case starts in the High Court. The SQE1 answer must fit the facts, the procedural or transactional stage, and any professional conduct overlay.
12 B Court structure This is a longer fact-pattern drill. The correct method is to spot Court structure, resist the trap (Assuming every important case starts in the High Court.), and choose the best legally available step.
13 A Human rights The trap is: Applying human rights analysis to a purely private dispute without a public law route. The SQE1 answer must fit the facts, the procedural or transactional stage, and any professional conduct overlay.
14 B Human rights The trap is: Applying human rights analysis to a purely private dispute without a public law route. The SQE1 answer must fit the facts, the procedural or transactional stage, and any professional conduct overlay.
15 C Human rights This is a longer fact-pattern drill. The correct method is to spot Human rights, resist the trap (Applying human rights analysis to a purely private dispute without a public law route.), and choose the best legally available step.
16 B ADR and settlement The trap is: Issuing proceedings before considering client objective and proportionality. The SQE1 answer must fit the facts, the procedural or transactional stage, and any professional conduct overlay.
17 C ADR and settlement The trap is: Issuing proceedings before considering client objective and proportionality. The SQE1 answer must fit the facts, the procedural or transactional stage, and any professional conduct overlay.
18 D ADR and settlement This is a longer fact-pattern drill. The correct method is to spot ADR and settlement, resist the trap (Issuing proceedings before considering client objective and proportionality.), and choose the best legally available step.

Q1. Client care

A client scenario in Legal Services and Professional Conduct contains the following clues: retainer, costs estimate, complaint, vulnerable client. Which option is the best SQE1 method?

  1. Take the step the client prefers because client instructions decide the answer.
  2. Use the clues (retainer, costs estimate, complaint, vulnerable client) to apply this rule: The client must understand scope, costs, complaints route and who is responsible for the matter.
  3. Identify the precise rule, apply it to the stated facts, and check procedure and ethics before selecting the best answer.
  4. Use the Korean-law equivalent unless the question expressly warns that England and Wales differs.
  5. Delay the answer because SQE1 questions never require practical advice.

Legal Services and Professional Conduct Questions 7-9

Q7. Conflicts

A client scenario in Legal Services and Professional Conduct contains the following clues: two clients, lender and borrower, personal interest. Which option is the best SQE1 method?

  1. Take the step the client prefers because client instructions decide the answer.
  2. Choose the answer that states a broad legal principle without testing the facts.
  3. Identify the precise rule, apply it to the stated facts, and check procedure and ethics before selecting the best answer.
  4. Use the clues (two clients, lender and borrower, personal interest) to apply this rule: Check own-interest conflict and client conflict before acting, then consider whether any exception genuinely applies.

Workbook Chapter 3. Constitutional and Administrative Law and EU Law

이 장은 Constitutional and Administrative Law and EU Law 문제풀이 장입니다. 목표는 지식을 많이 읽는 것이 아니라, 제한시간 안에서 trigger를 보고 바로 rule을 꺼내는 것입니다.

오늘의 목표

  1. 핵심 쟁점 6개를 문제로 확인한다.
  2. 짧은 issue drill과 긴 fact-pattern drill을 모두 푼다.
  3. 오답을 R/F/E/P/ETH 코드로 분류한다.
문항은 모두 새로 만든 연습문제입니다. 공식 sample question이나 유료 문제은행의 문항·선택지·해설을 복제하지 않습니다.

정답표입니다. 맞힌 문제도 해설을 읽고, 왜 다른 선택지가 best answer가 아닌지 한 문장으로 말합니다.

No.AnsIssueTeaching explanation
1 B Formation The trap is: Treating every negotiation statement as an offer. The SQE1 answer must fit the facts, the procedural or transactional stage, and any professional conduct overlay.
2 C Formation The trap is: Treating every negotiation statement as an offer. The SQE1 answer must fit the facts, the procedural or transactional stage, and any professional conduct overlay.
3 D Formation This is a longer fact-pattern drill. The correct method is to spot Formation, resist the trap (Treating every negotiation statement as an offer.), and choose the best legally available step.
4 C Terms The trap is: Calling every important term a condition. The SQE1 answer must fit the facts, the procedural or transactional stage, and any professional conduct overlay.
5 D Terms The trap is: Calling every important term a condition. The SQE1 answer must fit the facts, the procedural or transactional stage, and any professional conduct overlay.
6 E Terms This is a longer fact-pattern drill. The correct method is to spot Terms, resist the trap (Calling every important term a condition.), and choose the best legally available step.
7 D Exclusion clauses The trap is: Applying the clause before asking whether it became part of the contract. The SQE1 answer must fit the facts, the procedural or transactional stage, and any professional conduct overlay.
8 E Exclusion clauses The trap is: Applying the clause before asking whether it became part of the contract. The SQE1 answer must fit the facts, the procedural or transactional stage, and any professional conduct overlay.
9 A Exclusion clauses This is a longer fact-pattern drill. The correct method is to spot Exclusion clauses, resist the trap (Applying the clause before asking whether it became part of the contract.), and choose the best legally available step.
10 E Misrepresentation The trap is: Confusing a broken promise with a misrepresentation. The SQE1 answer must fit the facts, the procedural or transactional stage, and any professional conduct overlay.
11 A Misrepresentation The trap is: Confusing a broken promise with a misrepresentation. The SQE1 answer must fit the facts, the procedural or transactional stage, and any professional conduct overlay.
12 B Misrepresentation This is a longer fact-pattern drill. The correct method is to spot Misrepresentation, resist the trap (Confusing a broken promise with a misrepresentation.), and choose the best legally available step.
13 A Discharge The trap is: Using frustration for a merely more expensive bargain. The SQE1 answer must fit the facts, the procedural or transactional stage, and any professional conduct overlay.
14 B Discharge The trap is: Using frustration for a merely more expensive bargain. The SQE1 answer must fit the facts, the procedural or transactional stage, and any professional conduct overlay.
15 C Discharge This is a longer fact-pattern drill. The correct method is to spot Discharge, resist the trap (Using frustration for a merely more expensive bargain.), and choose the best legally available step.
16 B Damages The trap is: Awarding every foreseeable commercial loss without checking remoteness. The SQE1 answer must fit the facts, the procedural or transactional stage, and any professional conduct overlay.
17 C Damages The trap is: Awarding every foreseeable commercial loss without checking remoteness. The SQE1 answer must fit the facts, the procedural or transactional stage, and any professional conduct overlay.
18 D Damages This is a longer fact-pattern drill. The correct method is to spot Damages, resist the trap (Awarding every foreseeable commercial loss without checking remoteness.), and choose the best legally available step.

Workbook Chapter 8. Land Law

이 장은 Land Law 문제풀이 장입니다. 목표는 지식을 많이 읽는 것이 아니라, 제한시간 안에서 trigger를 보고 바로 rule을 꺼내는 것입니다.

오늘의 목표

  1. 핵심 쟁점 6개를 문제로 확인한다.
  2. 짧은 issue drill과 긴 fact-pattern drill을 모두 푼다.
  3. 오답을 R/F/E/P/ETH 코드로 분류한다.
문항은 모두 새로 만든 연습문제입니다. 공식 sample question이나 유료 문제은행의 문항·선택지·해설을 복제하지 않습니다.

1 B Instructions and client care The trap is: Starting searches before confirming who the client is. The SQE1 answer must fit the facts, the procedural or transactional stage, and any professional conduct overlay.

7 D Exchange The trap is: Assuming either party can withdraw after exchange without consequence. The SQE1 answer must fit the facts, the procedural or transactional stage, and any professional conduct overlay.
8 E Exchange The trap is: Assuming either party can withdraw after exchange without consequence. The SQE1 answer must fit the facts, the procedural or transactional stage, and any professional conduct overlay.
9 A Exchange This is a longer fact-pattern drill. The correct method is to spot Exchange, resist the trap (Assuming either party can withdraw after exchange without consequence.), and choose the best legally available step.
10 E Completion The trap is: Giving an undertaking without control over performance. The SQE1 answer must fit the facts, the procedural or transactional stage, and any professional conduct overlay.
11 A Completion The trap is: Giving an undertaking without control over performance. The SQE1 answer must fit the facts, the procedural or transactional stage, and any professional conduct overlay.
12 B Completion This is a longer fact-pattern drill. The correct method is to spot Completion, resist the trap (Giving an undertaking without control over performance.), and choose the best legally available step.
13 A Post-completion The trap is: Thinking the matter ends when keys are released. The SQE1 answer must fit the facts, the procedural or transactional stage, and any professional conduct overlay.

Workbook Chapter 13. Criminal Liability

이 장은 Criminal Liability 문제풀이 장입니다. 목표는 지식을 많이 읽는 것이 아니라, 제한시간 안에서 trigger를 보고 바로 rule을 꺼내는 것입니다.

오늘의 목표

  1. 핵심 쟁점 6개를 문제로 확인한다.
  2. 짧은 issue drill과 긴 fact-pattern drill을 모두 푼다.
  3. 오답을 R/F/E/P/ETH 코드로 분류한다.
문항은 모두 새로 만든 연습문제입니다. 공식 sample question이나 유료 문제은행의 문항·선택지·해설을 복제하지 않습니다.

Workbook Chapter 14. Criminal Law and Practice

이 장은 Criminal Law and Practice 문제풀이 장입니다. 목표는 지식을 많이 읽는 것이 아니라, 제한시간 안에서 trigger를 보고 바로 rule을 꺼내는 것입니다.

오늘의 목표

  1. 핵심 쟁점 6개를 문제로 확인한다.
  2. 짧은 issue drill과 긴 fact-pattern drill을 모두 푼다.
  3. 오답을 R/F/E/P/ETH 코드로 분류한다.
문항은 모두 새로 만든 연습문제입니다. 공식 sample question이나 유료 문제은행의 문항·선택지·해설을 복제하지 않습니다.

FLK2 Full Timed Mock Set

이 mock set은 FLK2 과목군에서 뽑은 180개 original 문제입니다. 공식 문항을 복제하지 않고, 이 문제집의 rule bank에서 재구성했습니다.

훈련 시간: 실제 구조에 맞춰 90문항 세션 2개로 풉니다. 각 세션은 2시간 33분, 평균 1.7분/문항 기준입니다.

규칙: 1회독에서는 멈추지 말고 90문항 세션을 끝까지 풉니다. 채점 후 R/F/E/P/ETH 분포를 보고 다음 주 공부 배분을 바꿉니다.
